On this Page

CRM/Agent Desk Post Message Events

The Expertflow CX sends following events to CRM via JavaScript post messages when CRM integration is enabled in agent desk settings.
       

USE CASE

AGENT DESK EVENTS 

Intended Attributes

QUESTIONS

1

State
JavaScript
"state": { 
   "name": "READY", 
   "reasonCode": null }

possible states :

  • READY 

  • NOT_READY

  • LOGOUT

  • LOGIN

Diference between objects ofAgent state change and Mrd state change?
If the value of this attribue "agentStateChanged" is true,Then Agent state changed,if false then Mrd state is changed.

State
JavaScript
"state": { 
"name": "READY",
"reasonCode": null }

possible states :

  • READY 

  • NOT_READY

  • BUSY

  • ACTIVE

  • PENDING_NOT_READY

  • Different Agent and MRD State Change? (yes)

3

  •  Is Conversation Id or Customer Id required in payload?
    (will send both ids)


External CRM/Systems can send the following commands to EFCX to change the agent/MRD state. In response to these commands, the system will send the agentPresence event.

USE CASE

Commands

QUESTIONS

1

To change Agent State


change agent state 
{
    event:"Connector_Action",
    agentData:{
        action:"agentStateChange",
        agentId:"<id>",
        state: { name: "<state>", reasonCode: null }

}


Required Data From CRM:

  • Required action i.e agentStateChange

  • Agent ID

  • Intended Agent State

2

To change MRD State


change MRD
JavaScript
{
    event:"Connector_Action",
    agentData:{
        action:"mrdStateChange",
        mrdId:"<mrd-id>"
        agentId:"<id>",
        state: { name: "<state>", reasonCode: null }

}


Required Data From CRM:

  • Required action i.e mrdStateChange

  • MRD ID

  • Agent ID

  • Intended MRD State
